A Train on the Beining Railway Derails in Tanggu

Caused by Excessive Speed

Tianjin News: Around 11:00 AM yesterday (the 20th), a troop train on the Beining Railway derailed in Tanggu while leaving the station. The cause of the derailment was that the train was eager to proceed and was traveling relatively fast. Furthermore, because it was carrying too little weight, the station procedures were completely in order when it left the station, and all safety signals had been lowered, so the driver confidently proceeded. Unexpectedly, the switch at the station entrance had a slight separation at the point where the rails connected. The train, carrying too little weight, was slightly bumpy and caused the separation to widen. The small wheels at the front of the locomotive derailed, followed by the large wheels at the rear. There were twelve cars behind the locomotive, and the pushing force was very strong, making it impossible to stop, causing the locomotive to derail and move forward several feet. Four of the boxcars directly behind the locomotive also derailed. Fortunately, the ground was sandy, so the wheels of the locomotive sank into the soil and did not overturn. One of the boxcars in the front overturned. Seeing the locomotive derail, several soldiers jumped off the train, resulting in six or seven injuries. The most seriously injured person died after being admitted to the Beining Hospital. The soldiers on the train, fearing that someone had deliberately sabotaged the railway and caused the derailment, temporarily disembarked to take precautions and fired their guns as a warning. The station personnel, fearing for their safety, fled. The station police officers tried to maintain order but were beaten by the soldiers. Later, the stationmaster and local police came forward to mediate. The station provided another locomotive and a freight car to move the undamaged cars back into the station. A temporary detour was built at the site of the derailment and completed at 3:00 PM, allowing the soldiers to continue west. A total of eight rails and over thirty ties were destroyed at the site of the derailment. None of the vehicles were completely destroyed. The total loss was only over two thousand yuan. After the detour was completed, all passenger trains resumed normal operations, but westbound trains were slightly delayed. (Dated the 21st)

Lu Bandits Flee North to Xintai

Burning and Killing Villages is Extremely Tragic

Jinan Correspondence: The bandit gang of Guo Maofeng in southern Shandong has fled north to Xintai, harassing Chenjiayu, twenty miles from the city. Han Fuju, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, telegraphed Wang Wanqing's troops, the Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Shandong Militia, and Tang Yaoxun's Brigade stationed in Qufu, to strictly suppress them. It is now reported that Chenjiayu Mountain Village and its blockhouse have been captured, and over a hundred villagers, male and female, have died. The number of those kidnapped and missing is not yet counted. The bandits, numbering over 1,500, have fled back to Mengshan in one group, and another group has plundered north of Xintai City and occupied Xinpu Mountain. After passing through Ruishan, Huangshangou, and other villages, they carried out large-scale burning and killing. On the 19th, they captured Gao Yaitou and Zhaojiazhuang, and the village leaders were disemboweled and flayed, which was extremely cruel. This group of bandits is still entrenched in the two villages, besieging nearby villages. Every night, they patrol on horseback, attacking people and burning villages. For days, the fires have been raging and corpses litter the roads. The postal route from Taian to Xintai and Mengyin is also blocked. The county seat is surrounded on three sides and in imminent danger. Yesterday (the 21st), representatives from various agencies in the county risked their lives to come to the province and urgently appealed to the provincial government headquarters for help. It is reported that Chairman Han has promised to send troops to suppress them immediately. (Dated the 22nd)

Qingdao Stock Exchange's Policy of Aggression Against China

Zhensheng & Co. Imitates Old Tricks of Dasugi & Co.

Chinese Merchants Plan to Establish Another Trading Organization

Qingdao Correspondence: The Qingdao Stock Exchange had a dispute caused by the loss of credit by the Japanese merchant Zhensheng & Co. After the Exchange's Sino-Japanese committee handled the punishment, it seemed to be over. An investigation revealed that the Exchange has a total of 36,000 shares, of which 18,111 are Chinese shares and 17,889 are Japanese shares. Opium King Liu Zishan alone occupies half of the Chinese shares. According to a businessman, ten years ago, the Japanese company Dasugi & Co., trading in raw oil, had a similar incident to what happened with Zhensheng & Co. After mediation, they were only fined two jiao per hundred jin, totaling a huge sum of 170,000 yuan. The ambition of the Japanese to manipulate the city's commerce is evident. After Dasugi & Co. was fined, it was almost bankrupt. The Japanese committee proposed relief, stipulating that all those trading at the Exchange from then on would have to pay a special fee. For example, oil would have a fee of one yuan and two jiao per hundred jin, later increased from one yuan and two jiao to two yuan and four jiao. Other goods were also subject to fees. The revenue from this special fee was used to compensate for the losses of Dasugi & Co. Over the past ten years, the fine of 170,000 yuan has only been reduced by a few thousand yuan, and it will be fully paid off this year. This alone shows that the Japanese policy of aggression against Qingdao's commerce is truly frightening. This time, Zhensheng & Co. imitated the old tricks of Dasugi & Co., hoping to manipulate the native product merchants to achieve its monopoly plan. Even if it fails, it can still rely on the Exchange's special income to compensate for its losses. The Japanese plan is indeed cunning. It is reported that the Sino-Japanese committee met on the 18th and decided on the punishment: the first transaction would be punished at 3%, totaling 5,544 yuan; the second would be punished at 300 yuan per hundred tons, totaling 2,850 yuan; and it was also decided that if such breaches of contract occur again in the future, they would be handled by fining one yuan per hundred yuan. The Exchange is scheduled to hold a shareholders' meeting on the 26th of this month to discuss and revise the salaries of Japanese staff and transaction deductions. It is also heard that Chinese merchants are indignant at the Exchange's multiple oppressions, so they plan to unite and establish another trading organization to counter and develop. It is currently under discussion. (Dated June 19th)

Recent Panic Scene in Shanxi Province

The Price of Paper Money Plummets Again

Drought Situation in Southern Shanxi

Taiyuan Correspondence: The problem of supplies for the troops stationed in southern Shanxi is being handled by the committee sent by the Deputy Commander's Office to distribute funds. However, the funds have not yet arrived in full. Even if they are distributed, the burden on the local area, which bears half the cost, is still difficult to avoid. Recently, a drought has developed in southern Shanxi, and grain prices have soared. The monthly salary of a few yuan for each soldier is not enough to live on. Representatives from Hedong, such as Jing Meijiu, have repeatedly negotiated with Song Zheyuan and others in recent days. However, it is still difficult to reach a proper decision before Shang Zhen returns to Taiyuan. Although there are rumors about the distribution of army salaries, according to military personnel, after Shang Zhen and others made various arrangements, they only distributed the arrears for December of last year and January and February of this year, adding 60% in Shanxi paper money. Only a certain amount of maintenance fees was issued for April. Nothing has been moved for March and May. Therefore, in reality, they are still in arrears for more than three months. Regarding the current situation of the armies, the generals have agreed to urge Xu Yongchang to take full responsibility for overall planning and rectification. Li Shengda, who went to Beiping to meet Zhang, returned to Taiyuan yesterday. Wang Jingguo will also return tonight. It is expected that the generals will have another meeting soon. Regarding the issue of Shanxi paper money, the price of the money has fallen further instead of rising in any way after the provincial government announced measures to maintain the price at 25%. The reason for the sharp decline is that it is related to the strength of the paper money itself and that rumors are also arising. What is most noteworthy about the current situation in Shanxi, apart from military and political affairs, is the drought situation in southern Shanxi. According to those who came from the disaster area, the wheat harvest this year is at most one dou per mu, and in many cases, even the seeds were not harvested. Less than 20-30% of the autumn crops have been planted. Recently, due to the prolonged drought without rain, even the small portion of seedlings that have been planted have withered. It is hopeless for the autumn harvest, so the food situation is presenting an extremely alarming scene. (Dated the 19th)

Japanese Government Officials in Korea Strictly Suppress Overseas Chinese Laborers

Korean Correspondence: Overseas Chinese in Japan and Korea have long been subjected to unfair treatment. The Japanese side has imposed extremely strict restrictions on overseas Chinese entering the country. In the past, overseas Chinese going to Japan had to follow the example of paying deposits and other inspection procedures before being allowed to reside. Since this year, even if they follow their harsh examples, they are not allowed to land. In Korea, in the 16th year of the Republic of China, the Japanese incited Koreans to form gangs and expel overseas Chinese. At that time, countless compatriots were killed and injured, and the loss of property was worth more than five million yuan. Although the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has repeatedly protested, the Japanese have ignored them, and it is still an outstanding case. Recently, they have been actively implementing expulsion policies, such as whipping and arresting, or forcibly fining, etc. The government officials have also strictly ordered the acquisition of permits. Only those with permits are allowed to reside, but when applying for permits, various interrogations are imposed, and as a result, permits often cannot be obtained, only insults.

In Incheon, overseas Chinese farmers and workers are expelled from the country if they do not have a residence permit outside their place of residence. On May 10 this year, the Japanese police station successively detained Bi Junrong, Li Qingde, Jiang Yunfeng, and others. They were first fined 20 yuan, but the farmers and workers were poor and unable to bear the fine, so they were imprisoned and beaten by the police station. The Incheon Sixth Branch of the Chinese Nationalist Party's directly affiliated branch in Korea sent personnel to accompany the director of the Incheon office of the Consulate General of Korea to protest to the Japanese government officials, but there has been no substantial result to date. Therefore, people are panicked, and many have returned to the country in succession.

Niaochiwon, Chungcheongnam-do

On May 10 this year, a Chinese worker surnamed Wang, who had obtained a permit from Honmachi, Gyeongseong, came here with a Japanese man to work at Izumi Kaido. Seven or eight days later, he was seen by the Japanese police, who first told the Japanese foreman that those who did not have permission from the police station here (i.e., the Niaochiwon police station) could not work here, and urged him to leave the country twice. Because the Chinese worker was not very familiar with the language, he did not leave immediately. The Japanese foreman did not explain the actual situation to him. On the 31st of last month, he was suddenly summoned to the police station and accused of not obeying the police station's orders and staying without permission, and had to admit a fine. Wang was unable to admit the fine and had no choice but to flee the country. His whereabouts are currently unknown.

Gaeseong

The more than 70 Chinese workers in this area are mostly engaged in agriculture, carpentry, or stonework. They are diligent and frugal and have long been praised by Japanese employers. On May 23 this year, the local police station suddenly sent police officers to Liu Chongli, Liu Xuelun, Yu Shugui, Wang Hongzhi, Zhou Yanchi, Li Shizhong, and 50 other Chinese workers to demand verification of their permits. The Chinese workers Liu Chongli and others said that they had not been notified in advance that they must obtain a permit before they could reside here. Now that they are suddenly asking for a permit, where can they get it? It is clear that they want to implement a crackdown. Later, the Chinese workers jointly requested the local police station to obtain a permit, but they ignored them. They still ordered them to return to the country three times a day. If they did not leave by the deadline, they would be fined or arrested. Now, Liu Chongli and 56 others have no hope of residing and cannot afford the cost of returning to their country, so they are in a dilemma and extremely distressed. They hope that our government and compatriots across the country will provide relief.

The above situations can be used as evidence of unequal treatment. There are not few Japanese people who come to China to work. Customs in various places often do not inspect them and allow them to land freely. They have always been treated with hospitality and have never been discriminated against. However, Japan's treatment of our overseas Chinese workers is so severely suppressed. Where is the so-called amity?

Changsha Qunzhi Students Destroy Newspaper Office

Changsha Correspondence: The Xiangjiang Evening News in this city has only been published for more than two months. On June 3, the newspaper published a news item entitled "Diplomas That Money Cannot Buy." On the 4th, it published a commentary entitled "Is This What Young People Should Be Like?" The article criticized a certain school of law and political science, Hunan Qunzhi School of Law and Political Science (i.e., the parent school of the Shanghai Qunzhi School). The students believed that the "certain school of law and political science" referred to in the newspaper was their school, and that the school did not sell diplomas. The newspaper published information that damaged the reputation of the school. On the afternoon of June 19, more than 50 students gathered and rushed into the editorial department of the Xiangjiang Evening News at Gaoshengmen, asking questions and demanding the surrender of the contributor. At that time, only the newspaper's manager, Tang Jin, and the distributor, Li Jianxun, were at the office. They came out to negotiate and advised them to use written procedures to make corrections. The students ignored them, slammed the table, and dragged Tang and Li to the Lezhongcun printing office (i.e., the newspaper's printing location) and took away all the old and new drafts. After the search, they dragged Tang and Li back to the school for disposal. When they were dragged to the Shuidao Lane intersection, the patrol team of the North Third Precinct Police Station heard the news and arrived to stop them. The students dispersed in a burst. Only Deng Qun, the student who led the team, was arrested on the spot. Tang and Li were rescued immediately. The patrol team took Deng back to the North Third Precinct Police Station for disposal. While they were questioning him, dozens of students from the school gathered again and surrounded the police station, demanding the release of Deng Qun. At this time, Mao Fengxiang, the editor of the Xiangjiang Evening News, heard the news and rushed to the police station. The students surrounded Mao again. Before long, Wang Shouren, an adjutant from the Garrison Headquarters, led a platoon of armed soldiers to rush to the scene to suppress them. He, along with the patrol officer Huang Kun from the police station, gave guidance in various ways. The students then lined up and returned to school, leaving Deng Qun, the newspaper's manager Tang Jin, editor Mao Fengxiang, and clerk Li Jianxun to be sent to the North District Police Station. Chief Li interrogated them clearly, and when they determined that the case was a criminal matter, the police station had no right to handle it. He ordered them all to be released on bail and told them to appeal to the competent authorities. After Tang, Mao, and the others returned to the office, they saw that the belongings had been destroyed and the drafts at the printing office had been lost. It was impossible to publish temporarily, so they temporarily suspended publication from June 20. On the one hand, they reported to the provincial party headquarters, the provincial government, the garrison headquarters, the public security bureau, and the education department to request investigation and handling. On the other hand, they reported to the Journalists Association and requested that they uphold justice. It is not yet known how it will be resolved. (Dated June 20)

Wuxi

Drug Offenders Convicted and Fined Separately

Last month, in the Wang Qiaoxian brothel outside the North Gate of Chang'an Bridge, retired abbot Pu Qing of the Longguang Temple in Xishan and others were found smoking opium. The police chief of the Fifth Public Security Sub-bureau arrested them at the scene. Chief Peng of the Sub-bureau presented the prostitute Chen Jujuan and Pu Qing et al. to the County Public Security Bureau, which transferred them to the County Court. Chief Judge Zhou conducted the trial and released them on bail. Recently, Chen Jujuan appeared in court, but the monk Pu Qing repeatedly failed to appear. The original guarantor, Chen Baoshu, was detained and given a deadline to produce him, but he still did not appear. Yesterday, Yang, the acting judge, sentenced Chen Jujuan to one month of imprisonment and a fine of two hundred yuan for the opium case. After the appeal period, she will be sent to the detention center to serve her sentence. Also, Xu Zhengzhi, a private seller of red pills, was sentenced by Judge Liang yesterday to one year of imprisonment and a fine of two hundred yuan. Cao Wanlong was fined one hundred yuan and sentenced to six months of imprisonment. Furthermore, the opium offender Li Chen was sentenced by Judge Liang to two months of imprisonment and a fine of ten yuan, and Zhang Feng was sentenced to two months of imprisonment and a fine of twenty yuan. He Fushou and Hu Jintang were each sentenced to one month of imprisonment by Acting Judge Yang. Moreover, Huang Lao San, a seller of red pills, obtained five catties and four ounces of red pills in Shanghai the day before yesterday. He arrived in Wuxi late at night, and the porter Cao Shoushan secretly took some. Huang Xin was unwilling and gathered more than a dozen hooligans to demand it back, but failed, resulting in a violent fight. Cao's head was smashed by the hooligans, and he was bleeding profusely. The patrolling police arrived and dispersed the hooligans, detaining both sides and sending them to the County Court. Chief Judge Zhou opened the court, examined Cao Shoushan's injuries, and ordered him to return home for treatment. Huang Lao San was detained for further investigation.

Police Officer's Affair Reported to the Department for Instructions

Sun Rongding, the chief of the Second Public Security Sub-bureau of Guangfu Gate in our county, was caught in room 25 of the Qitai Inn on the road having illicit relations with a young woman named Tang Quanyu by Wei Mei and Zou Tingliang. This has already been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that County Magistrate Pan Zhongjia was furious after reading the report and immediately telegraphed Director Xu to report the incident voluntarily. After receiving the order, Director Xu prepared a document and submitted it to the County Government, which was then forwarded to the Department of Civil Affairs for instructions. It is unknown how Director Hu will handle the matter.

New Twists in the Silk Industry Relief Public Bond

The Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui silk industry relief public bond, previously decided by the government to be eight million yuan, was intended to use one-fourth to improve sericulture, one-fourth to reorganize machinery, and two-fourths to encourage raw silk exports and provide relief to the silk industry. Both the management and custody committees were organized early to take charge of the matter. However, after more than a year, the public bond has not been issued. All silk mills in Wuxi believe that the investigation procedures of silk reeling machines and silk inventory in Wuxi have been completed. However, the customs surcharge for the public bond fund has been in effect for one month, and the organization of the management committee has been established for more than half a month, but the public bond has not been issued, and the fund is still being collected, ostensibly providing relief to silk merchants but actually increasing their burden. If the relief funds are not issued as before, this fund should be submitted to the central government for temporary suspension of collection. Yesterday, the silk industry association reported to the management committee to forward the request to the central government to order the Jianghai Customs to temporarily suspend the collection of the public bond fund to protect the silk industry.

Changzhou

Shipping Boat Robbed in Shen Port

A boat sailing from Jiangyin to Changzhou was robbed on the evening of the 21st in the Jiangjiawan area of Sanhekou. Liu Bixiao Fang, the owner's brother, was burned, and He Canbao, a crew member, was shot and wounded. The robbers then plundered the boat and left. On the 22nd, the victim rescued the injured and reported the case to the county government, requesting an arrest.

Labor Strike at Shenxin No. 6 Factory

After the Changzhou Yarn Factory outside Xiaonanmen in Wujin was closed, it was managed by the Shanghai Creditors' Group. In 1927, Rong E’sheng from Wuxi leased and opened the Shenxin No. 6 Yarn Factory, which has been in operation for five years and has earned a profit of approximately 880,000. Now, the Changzhou Yarn Factory Creditors' Group has decided to take it back and manage it themselves, renaming it Minfeng Company. They notified Shenxin that they would take over at the end of this month, and Minfeng will open on July 1st. Shenxin has over 1,400 male and female workers. Upon hearing this news, they went on strike unanimously on the 22nd and put forward four demands: (1) All male and female workers should be paid six months' worth of severance pay from the date of dismissal; (2) Bonuses and leftover materials in the factory should be distributed in full without any deduction; (3) All workers' unpaid wages for the previous half-month should be returned in full from the date of the strike without retention; (4) Wages should be paid as usual during the strike. The factory feared an incident and requested the Public Security Bureau to send police to maintain order. Sun Fukang, the chief inspector of the Public Security Bureau, led the police to the factory and instructed the workers to elect representatives to negotiate. The workers demanded that the six months' severance pay should be allocated by the factory and deposited in the County Party Department and Public Security Bureau to show good faith, and said that the four demands were all based on the example of the Dachang Yarn Factory's dismissal and were not excessive. Chief Inspector Sun promised to forward the demands to Manager Rong Esheng for discussion and announced that representatives from the workers, the factory, and the Public Security Bureau would be sent to investigate and verify. By around 7:00 PM, most of the female workers had returned home, leaving 300 to 400 people to guard the goods in the factory and maintain order together with the factory police, awaiting a resolution. According to news this morning (the 23rd), both parties are still negotiating.

Changshu

New Finance Bureau Chief Takes Office

Hao Bingzhang, the Finance Bureau Chief of our county, was transferred to the province. Zhuang Yeguang, the Finance Bureau Chief of Wuxi, was appointed to fill the vacancy. The new Chief Zhuang arrived in Changshu on the 22nd and will officially take office on the 24th. It is said that there will be some changes in the bureau's staff.

Eight Fishing Boats Robbed in Dongxing Sand

In Fushan Port, the eighth district, this year's hairtail fishing season is still quite good. There are about forty to fifty fishing boats of all sizes, but it is still not as good as Hupu Port. Recently, the hairtail season is coming to an end, and the fishing boats are planning to return together. Unexpectedly, pirates are taking advantage of the opportunity of the fishing boats returning and becoming rampant again. On the 20th, a large group of hairtail fishing boats from Hupu Port, about a hundred or so, left the port. While passing through the Dongxingsha sea entrance, they were suddenly followed by three pirate ships, which fired shots as a warning. The group knew they had encountered pirates and fled. The pirates fired shots and chased after them, resulting in eight fishing boats being intercepted and robbed. There are now dozens of fishing boats from Jiangbei or Chongming anchored there, all feeling uneasy. On the 21st, the Zhenyu patrol warship stationed in Hupu happened to be patrolling to the entrance of Fushan. The boat owners all requested the warship to protect them on their return journey. The captain of the warship approved the request and decided to escort them out of the county to avoid danger on the way.

Jiangyin

Local Budget Meeting for Fiscal Year 20

The county government convened a meeting of various agencies on the afternoon of the 22nd to discuss the local budget for fiscal year 20. After discussion, it was found that the local funds for fiscal year 19 had a deficit of more than 130,000. Even if all items were paid at 85% of their listed amounts, it would still be difficult to balance income and expenditure. A decision was made on the principles of expenditure without a method for clearing the deficit: (1) No new projects should be added in fiscal year 20; (2) Existing expenses should be tightened as much as possible; (3) Clear arrears, reorganize the busy season tax collection, issue local treasury bills, and request subsidies from the provincial government; (4) The expenses of the district offices should still be paid at 50%; (5) The expenses of the Public Security Bureau should be independently managed starting from fiscal year 20; (6) The monthly subsidy of 200 yuan to Qingyang Junior High School should be reported back to the Education Department as difficult to subsidize; (7) The county government gazette should be tentatively set at 50 yuan per month.

Yangzhou

Military Governor's Office Executes Red Bandit by Firing Squad

The Jiangsu Pacification Military Governor's Office, according to the Tonghai Pacification Sub-district Commander Shi Dexue, transferred a red bandit named Zhang Xingling from Rugao County to the office. The victim, Wu Zhongxiang, testified that the bandit led a group to burn and kill his father, Wu Shengwu, his dry sister, Wang Suyun, and the hired worker, Jiang Weikai, as true. The Military Governor's Office sent personnel to investigate with the county government. Zhang was confirmed to be the perpetrator who shot and killed Wu and Liu, and had led more than a hundred bandits to burn and loot Baimatang, Caojiabu, Yejitan, and other places. The bandit confessed that he had collected money from residents on behalf of the Red Army and led a group to burn, loot, and shoot many people. The Military Governor's Office sentenced him to death and, at 3:00 PM today, after confirming his identity, sent a team to escort him to the execution ground at the train station and executed him by firing squad.

Recently, in various parts of Jiangbei, the winter wheat has ripened, and all farmers are engaged in harvesting. Sui-Ning Bandit Gang Defeated

The Wei Yousan bandit gang entrenched in Baowei, Suining, was surrounded and severely suppressed by Commander Zhang Zhankui's troops. The bandits retreated towards Guirenji, Suqian. Subsequently, Brigade Commander Liu Guoming of the 95th Brigade led his troops from Siyang County to meet them and deliver a fierce blow, killing more than 20 bandits and capturing three fake platoon leaders, including Li Yifu, and seizing more than a dozen rapid-firing rifles. The bandits were unable to withstand the attacks and fled in two directions. One group fled to Xiaohu, and the other group fled to Zhouwei. The troops of Brigade Commander Liu and Commander Zhang are dividing their forces to track down and suppress the bandits, hoping to completely eliminate them.

Nantong

Tongzhou Cloth Industry Cracks Down on Weaving Households' Cheating

The Tongzhou Dachichi native cloth industry has recently suffered a major blow to its sales because the weaving households in the four townships are not seeking improvements but are cheating for profit. The industry has obtained approval from Party and government agencies to implement a crackdown on cheating. The county government has issued a notice with seven measures: (1) Any weaving household that mixes and sells cloth that has been treated with sizing, is damp, short, or has fake colors will not only be prevented from being bought by each village, but the cloth will also be detained and returned after the weaving household falls behind in payments; (2) For cloth with fake colors that is being sold in pawnshops and is not subject to inspection, the association will re-examine it, stamp it, and return it; (3) Weaving households that do not accept the punishment will be reported to the Public Security Bureau for handling; (4) All villages must not buy fake cloth; (5) All villages must not use other methods to punish fake cloth; (6) Villages that buy fake cloth indiscriminately will be punished by the association; (7) Cloth inspectors who are found to be colluding and engaging in corruption will be reported to the county government for punishment.

Sea Guerrilla Team's Operational Area Determined

The Provincial Security Department has reorganized Shen Fengshan's entire surrendered force of more than 500 men into a sea guerrilla team. It has already inspected them in Chibing Tea. The designated operational area for Shen's troops is the sea area belonging to Tongtai, which is responsible for arresting sea bandits. Their monthly salary will be issued by the province.

The Lusi Police Regiment arrested two bandits, Wang Hongfu and Zhang Pengchuan, who were carrying weapons and robbing. On the 22nd, they were sent to the county government for interrogation.

Robbery in Shiwan, Bandits Sent to Province for Interrogation

Verdict in Case of Resisting Arrest While Gambling

In late January of this year, farmers Zhu Yubing and others from Chongde County held a ritual for the completion of the new bridge, chanting scriptures and gambling. The nearby land police learned of this and went to arrest them. At that time, Zhu and others gathered a crowd to resist arrest, seized the police officers, removed their uniforms and symbols, and falsely reported to the stationed water police that bandits were robbing. The water police arrived at the scene, tied them up, and sent them to the district headquarters. The district headquarters investigated and found out the facts and released them all. The Chongde County Public Security Bureau subsequently arrested Zhu Liukun, who made a false report, and Zhu Yubing, Zhu Shunchang, and Fei Rufa, who gathered a crowd to obstruct official duties. After many twists and turns, Zhu and others hired lawyers to petition the High Court to transfer jurisdiction. The Jiaxing Branch Court was designated to hear the case. The verdict has now been announced yesterday. Zhu Liukun and others were each sentenced to three months of imprisonment.

Hangzhou

Rice Industry Granted Exemption from Business Tax

The business tax in various cities and counties of Zhejiang Province has been prepared for many months and was finally implemented this month. Various industries have requested exemptions, but because it concerns the tax revenue of the entire province, all requests have been rejected. However, the rice industry associations in various places, because the rice and grain industry is of great importance to the livelihood of the people, specially submitted a request to the provincial chamber of commerce, which forwarded it to the Finance Department for approval to exempt them from the tax. There has been no reply yet. Yesterday, the Rice Industry Federation of various counties publicly elected Ge Anfu as a representative to petition the Finance Department. It is now learned that Wang Xicun, the Director of the Finance Department, believes that the rice industry is related to the livelihood of the common people and is different from other industries, so he has decided to propose it to the provincial government meeting tomorrow for approval and issue a notice of exemption.

Bandits Rob and Are Caught on the Spot

Four or five bandits suddenly came to the Wang family in Tongjiang, southern Xiaoshan, on the night of the 20th and robbed the family of their clothes, ornaments, and miscellaneous items. Old Man in His Sixties Abducts Young Girl

The Rural Clearing Office in the seventh district of eastern Xiaoshan arrested an old man over sixty years old for abducting a seventeen-year-old girl, crossing the river to Xiaoshan. The office interrogated him and learned that the old man was a long-term worker of a certain family in the Sandi area of Haining, and the girl was the family's adopted daughter. The old man intended to abduct her to Shaoxing for sale, but the matter was discovered, and he confessed the truth. The office sent him to the County Court for legal action.

Unfilial Son Driven Away and Drowns Himself

Yu Jiuxing, the son of Yu Awei in the Shalangyu area of the Sandi in Western Xiaoshan, never engaged in honest work and specialized in gambling and wandering. Before the Dragon Boat Festival, he owed debts and was unable to pay them. He asked his old father for money. His father Awei hated him so much that he drove him away. Unexpectedly, after leaving, Jiuxing drowned himself in the river on the day of the Dragon Boat Festival. The next morning, his father heard the news and sent someone to retrieve the body. He was immediately buried in a coffin by the river.

Mingguang

Rampant Beach Bandits in Northwest Township

The large reed beach in the northwest township of our county, which surrounds more than a hundred li and is bordered by water on three sides, with reeds reaching the sky, has always been an area where bandits appear. Recently, it has been occupied by the notorious bandit Fan Xianxi. The bandit gang has about 400 people and is a remnant of the "Three Legs" gang. They are extremely rampant. Ships passing through their area are robbed. As a result, transportation in that area has been cut off. On the 12th of this month, the fifth police team, together with the nearby militia, launched a suppression campaign, only managing to recover more than 30 looted ships. On the 13th and 14th, the bandits openly burned and looted the villages of Mengjiatai, Dengjia’an, Yaozhuang, and Yaotai. On the 15th, they kidnapped nine men and women in the northern part of Panzcun, killing four. The surrounding areas are in a state of extreme panic.

Local

Various Schools Hold Graduation Ceremonies

Central University Medical School

The Medical School of Central University is one of the eight colleges of the National Central University under the Ministry of Education. Since its establishment, it has maintained excellent standards and outstanding achievements. This year, the first class of the college is graduating, with a total of twelve students. They were recruited as high school graduates and studied for two years in the pre-medical program before being promoted to the professional program. The professional program lasts five years. The first four years are for academic study, and the fifth year is spent at Shanghai Red Cross General Hospital, Nanjing Central Hospital, Shanghai Tongren Hospital, Suzhou Bo Xi Hospital, and other places for internships. Therefore, the time limit is longer than other departments. The graduation ceremony was held at 9:00 AM yesterday in the newly built auditorium of Nanjing Central University. The graduates were led to Beijing by Dean Yan Fuqing.

Renhe Midwifery School

The Renhe Midwifery School held its 18th graduation ceremony yesterday. Party Teachers Who Have Been Certified Must Still Complete Registration Procedures

丨The City Training Department Has Officially Announced 丨

The Shanghai Special City Party Department Training Department, in order to maintain the qualifications of Party instructors throughout the city

Committee for the Compilation of Curriculum and Equipment for Primary and Secondary Schools

丨 Detailed Record of the Second Meeting 丨

The records of the first meeting of the two groups of elementary and secondary schools of the Committee for the Compilation of Curriculum and Equipment Standards for Elementary and Secondary Schools convened by the Ministry of Education have already been seen in this newspaper on the 18th and 19th. As for the records of the second meeting, this newspaper only published the main points of the resolution. The official record of the second meeting of the committee is now reprinted below.

Middle School Group

The second meeting was held in the Ministry of Education conference hall on the 20th, morning and afternoon. Committee members present were Zhu Jingnong, Zhong Daochang, Tan Qifang, Zhao Zhengduo, Dai Yingguan, Gu Shusen, Zheng Hesheng, Li Qingsong, Xia Chengfeng, Sun Lianggong, Xu Yiqiao, Du Tingxiu, Ai Wei, Zhu Wenshu, Zhang Shiyi, Wang Maozu, Xie Shuying, Xu Zhunqi, and Lin Duanfu. Weng Zhida attended as an observer. Gu Shusen was the chairman, and Weng Zhida was the recorder. Formalities were observed. Report matters: 1. The chairman reported the resolutions of the first meeting. Discussion matters: Continued discussion of the Ministry of Education's opinions on middle school curriculum standards. "Resolutions": (1) The total number of credits for general science in senior high school was changed to 160. (2) The distribution of credits for each subject in senior high school general studies was changed as follows: Party Principles: 12 (original standard); Chinese Language: 24 (original standard); Foreign Language: 30; Mathematics: 15; National History: 6 (original standard); Foreign History: 6 (original standard); National Geography: 4; Foreign Geography: 4; Physics: 7; Chemistry: 7; Biology: 6; Military Training: 6 (original standard); Physical Education: 9 (original standard); Elective Courses: 24. (3) Senior high school general studies elective courses should be divided into three groups: the first group for liberal arts subjects, the second group for science subjects, and the third group for vocational subjects. Detailed subjects should be drafted by committee members of each group. The following committee members were appointed: First Group (Liberal Arts Subjects): Zhang Shiyi, Wang Maozu, Li Qingsong, Xia Chengfeng; Second Group (Science Subjects): Xie Shuying, Ai Wei, Tan Qifang; Third Group (Vocational Subjects): Wang Maozu, Zhu Jingnong, Xu Yiqiao, Zhong Daochang. (4) Starting from the third grade of junior high school, the curriculum should be divided into two types. The first type is the previously decided subjects and their credits, for students preparing to advance to higher education. The second type reduces non-essential subjects for those not advancing to higher education, or reduces their credits, and adds vocational subjects. Students not preparing for higher education will study this type. These students may also extend their study period by one year specifically for vocational training. (5) Vocational elective subjects in the second type of curriculum for the third grade of junior high school are set at 17 to 20 credits (compared to the first type of curriculum, reducing 10 credits in English, 3 credits in labor, plus the original 4 to 7 elective credits, totaling 17 to 20 credits). 2. The opinions of each committee member on the revision of each subject were submitted to the subject review committee for discussion. 3. This committee appointed subject committee members to be responsible for reviewing and revising the provisional standards of each subject curriculum. Subject committee members should appropriately include the original drafters and must include experts in each subject and those with practical educational experience. Among the senior high school subject reviewers, there should also be one university professor in charge of each subject. During the review, attention should be paid to ensuring that there are no omissions or repetitions in the curriculum connections between junior and senior high school, and senior high school and university. 4. The next meeting is scheduled to be held before July 15.

Elementary School Group

The second meeting was attended by committee members Hu Shuyi, Hu Yanli, Zhu Wenshu, Chen Heqin, Shen Baiying, Shi Renfu, Ma Ketan, Shen Leiyu, Jiang Xicen, Zhao Tingwei, Wu Yinyin, Peng Baichuan (Yinyin as representative), Xue Tianhan, and Li Qingsu. Wu Yinyin was the chairman, and Xue Tianhan was the recorder.

(1) Report Matters

Review reports from each group: 1. Chinese Language: (1) Lower the minimum limit. (2) Incorporate explanations of Party Principles materials into the selection criteria. (3) For semi-cursive script in middle grades, only recognition is required. (4) The National Phonetic Alphabet should only be placed in reading materials. (6) The total time should be changed to 330 minutes for grades 1 and 2, and 420 minutes for grades 3, 4, 5, and 6 (calculated with at least 30 minutes of reading per day). (6) Remove the section on supplementary reference books. (7) Change the silent reading speed within the minimum limit to 120 to 180 words per minute for primary level and 220 to 240 words per minute for advanced level. (8) The scope of stories cannot be determined; please submit for discussion. (9) Please submit the vocabulary list proposed for deletion from the lower limit for discussion. 2. Social Studies: (1) The goals and types of assignments have not changed much. (2) Cancel the hygiene section in the assignment requirements; add social knowledge that does not belong to history and geography. (3) Please submit for discussion whether to call social knowledge that does not belong to history and geography "civics." (4) The content of the assignment requirements has not changed much; however, general clauses have been changed to specific and listed ones. (5) The headings regarding nationalism, democracy, and people's livelihood were deleted because they are not easy to distinguish in practice. (6) Civics materials: Grades 1 and 2 are mostly Party Principles, social relationships, etiquette, public institution guard practice, love of living things, and love of public property. Grades 3 and 4 are the same, plus autonomous activities, practical practice, city and township organization research, and a general study of the Three Principles of the People. Grades 5 and 6 are the same, plus occupation, public entertainment, local autonomy, public service, world citizenship, simple economic system organization (such as cooperatives), and covenants. (7) The minimum limit for public health omissions should be supplemented. 3. Nature: (1) Remove the footnote from the objective. (2) Remove the hygiene section. (3) The assignment categories and assignment requirements have been slightly changed. (4) In the teaching method points, the phrase "use textbooks as a principle" is proposed to be deleted; please submit for discussion. (5) Most of the graduation minimum limit belongs to the hygiene section and should be revised in detail. 4. Arithmetic: (1) The objective and assignment categories have not changed much. (2) Some materials from business conditions that can be adopted have been added to the original items in the assignment requirements, and the arrangement of the before and after order has not changed much. (3) Add in the assignment requirements footnote: "Depending on local conditions, starting from the fourth or fifth grade, add abacus calculation appropriately, limited to 30 to 60 minutes per week" (calculated within the arithmetic time). Is this method appropriate? Please submit for discussion. 5. Work: (1) Change the name to Labor and incorporate business conditions and research sections into other subjects. (1) The business conditions in the assignment categories are clearer than the original standards, such as "Advanced Special Study of One or Two Types," etc. (3) Add rattan work to the assignment categories and incorporate wax work and plaster work into art. (4) Add a note under the assignment categories explaining the necessary measures for schools to set up a labor science department. (5) Delete points (1) and (2) of the teaching method points, and the rest have been slightly changed. (6) Lower the minimum limit (reduce the quantity and do not use cumulative totals). 6. Fine Arts: (1) Change the production item in the assignment categories to include drawing and adding notes (plaster and wax modeling). Change the word "production" to "presentation." (2) Add appreciation of natural scenery, still life sketching, and pattern painting to the assignment requirements. (3) Add the procedure for using tools to the twelfth item of the teaching method points. (4) Lower the minimum limit. 7. Health: Health and hygiene and physical education are merged, so the objectives are not divided. A. Physical Education: (1) Add simple national arts to the third parenthesis of the assignment categories. Add "and game competitions" (3) Incorporate the original standard's objectives into the training. (3) In the assignment requirements, add competitive games under imitation games for grades 1 and 2, and add track and field sports under sports items for grades 3 and 4. (3) In the teaching method points, (5) add the word "arrogance" under fraud. (6) "Without hindering school order" The fourteenth method of grouping athletes should be changed to "Intermediate and advanced levels are combined into six groups. For convenience, they are grouped according to weight. Schools may adjust according to actual circumstances. A. 60 pounds and above B. 80 pounds and above. C. 70 pounds and above. D. 60 pounds and above. E. 50 pounds and above. F. 50 pounds and below. The items changed in the sports items are as follows: A codes are changed to meters. B Add several track and field items. C Girls' grouping weight is compared with boys, and the competition items are reduced compared to boys. D Low-level cancellation of sports focuses on game competitions (4) Add in the teaching method points: 15 Game competition methods. (5) The McCurdy Motor Skill Standard is not suitable for class use; please submit for discussion. B. The health system is a newly created curriculum drafting process. The characteristics are as follows: (1) Not entirely related to the body (2) Add security aspects (3) Add both sexes (4) Pay special attention to mutual assistance in public health. 8. Music: (1) Add research on the structure and repair methods of ordinary musical instruments to the research item in the assignment categories. (2) Delete the beats and reading methods of work songs and 3/8 time from the assignment requirements for grades 3 and 4 and move them to grades 5 and 6. (3) Lower the minimum limit: all items in grades 4 and 5 of the primary level and 5 items in the advanced level are deleted, and the number of lyrics is also reduced. 9. Kindergarten: (1) Add one to the objective: increase the physical and mental health of young children. (2) In the main points of the work subject content, add paper pulp work under clay work.

According to the newly promulgated regulations of the Central Government, the qualification of party principles teachers must be reviewed, and the party principles teachers who have passed the examination should also register with the Qualification Review Committee of Party Principles Teachers to continue to maintain their qualifications. Now that the Qualification Review Committee of Party Principles Teachers in this city has already started working, the Municipal Training Department announced in the Republican Daily the other day that all party principles teachers of all levels of schools who have passed the first, second, third, and fourth examinations in the city should quickly register with the committee to meet the regulations and avoid losing their original qualifications. It is heard that the registration procedure is very simple, only requiring the filling out of a form, attaching three two-and-a-half-inch half-length photos, and submitting the certificate of examination. In the future, when the qualifications are organized and determined, the original qualifications will still be used as the standard. However, if one wants to obtain a higher level of qualification, one must follow the procedures for requesting a review and submit proof of academic qualifications and experience.

The Youth Association Reopens Summer School

The Youth Association in this port, as the general hub of the National Youth Association, has always paid great attention to the cultivation of cadre talents. It used to run a summer school in Lushan every summer, and the results were remarkable. Recently, it has been suspended for several years. It has now been decided to reopen it this summer, so that youth association cadres from all over the country have a place to rest and study. The school will be held from July 18 to August 15, and the location is still Lian Valley in Lushan, Jiangxi. The teachers who have been hired include Xie Fuya, Wu Zelin, Fu Ruoyu, Pan Guangdan, Gan Linge, Hou Enqing, Liang Shichun, Zheng Wei, Xie Songsan, and Mageli. They are all well-learned scholars who love education, psychology, society, and religion, and are rich in research and experience. The position of principal was originally scheduled to be taken by Mr. Li Xiaochu, the general secretary of the association. However, because Mr. Liang Junyan went to the Americas to attend the World Youth Conference, Mr. Fu Ruoyu, the dean of studies, has been asked to act as an agent. It is heard that many youth association cadres from all over the country have registered to join.

Sports

May Order Cancels Confrontation

Saying please postpone until September

丨Jiangnan Baihong Disappointed丨

For the track and field confrontation proposed by the American army Mai Lingsi, Jiangnan Baihong had planned to unite to participate in the war. They sent a letter to the American army, scheduled for the 28th. After receiving the letter, the American army suddenly replied yesterday, saying that all proposed track and field confrontation matters should be temporarily cancelled and postponed until September. Jiangnan Baihong was greatly disappointed after learning the news.

Track and Field Athletes Work Hard Jiangnan Scheduled to Northward Expedition

Take the bus north on the 27th

Return to Shanghai via Tianjin, Ping, Liaoning and Dalian

The Jiangnan Track and Field Team, which was formed after returning to China after the Far East failure, has achieved remarkable results in participating in various sports events and is well-known. In view of the strong atmosphere of track and field sports in North China, most of the results are also better than here, so take advantage of this summer vacation, and resolutely, the entire team of more than 30 people went north to explore and learn from each other.

Delay due to Northern Expedition

After Mai Ling challenged the Chinese team, the Association politely declined. Jiangnan originally planned to confront Mai Ling alone, and entrusted Zhou Jiaqi, the executive of the Association, to negotiate everything. The date was set for June 21. Later, the Association received a letter from Baihong, willing to compete with Mai Ling, so the confrontation between Jiangnan and Mai Ling was temporarily postponed, intending to unite the two teams to confront Mai Ling, in order to fulfill the wishes of both parties. It was scheduled to be held on the 28th, but Mai Ling unexpectedly cancelled the previous proposal for confrontation, not only disappointing the Jiangnan and Baihong teams, but also delaying the Jiangnan's Northern Expedition schedule.

Competition Schedule

It is now scheduled to depart by Jinghu train on the 27th of this month, stay in Yu Ning for one day, cross the river on the 29th, and go straight to Tianjin along the Jinpu Road. Stay at Nankai University. After the competition is over, go to Beiping in about six days, and plan to live in Tsinghua. At the latest by the 10th, pack up and go out to Liaoning. The residence is arranged by the Liaoning Provincial Track and Field Team (after the confrontation, plan to take the sea route back to Shanghai via Dalian.

Source of Funds

In addition to each team member bearing about 15 yuan, donations are being raised from all parties. Tan Yankai's son Tan Bi donated 200 yuan, Tan Bi donated 200 yuan, Cheng Yize donated 200 yuan, Huang Bohui donated 50 yuan, and the rest are being negotiated. The Municipal Government and the Municipal Education Bureau have been requested to allocate funds for subsidies.

The 55th World Tennis Championships

丨Opened a few days ago丨

Surprising丨Failure of French Ke Xian Tuo

Formidable丨Japanese Players All Active

London, 22nd - The 55th World Tennis Wimbledon Tennis Championships opened on the afternoon of the 22nd, with tens of thousands of viewers. As the war began, a surprising achievement was suddenly discovered, which was the failure of French star Ke Xian Tuo and the activity of Japanese players.

Ke Xian Tuo Eliminated After Illness

Ke Xian Tuo, a French star, was opposed by the British Nie Geer Shabao. Under the battle, the British Shabao was calm and skilled in shooting, making it difficult for the French star to cope. Ke Xian Tuo's full body skills lost his energy after his illness, and he sighed and left. The result was 1-6, 3-6, 2-6.

Japanese Players All Active

Japanese players who joined the competition are exceptionally active. Miki defeated Haddi 6-3, 6-4, and 6-2; Kawachi defeated Fei Zhi 6-0, 6-0, and 6-4; Sato Jiro defeated South African Gou Pei 6-3, 6-2, and 6-4; Aoki defeated Dou Pula Kesi 6-3, 6-3, and 6-3; Sato Hyotaro also entered the second week of competition without fighting due to the injury and abandonment of his opponent Magroof.

American Youth Ready to Win Championship

Although the American Iron Shield Dun is absent from this session, the championship is still very promising. Heroes are majestic and strong, and Sears, Rott, Ellison, Fan Ling, Wood, and Setho are all ready to win the championship. Sears defeated Spance 6-1, 6-1, and 6-2 without effort, and Fan Ling also eliminated Yugoslav Skivo 6-0, 6-2, and 6-1.

French Team Has Little Hope

Predictors say that France has little hope. Ke Xian Tuo has failed, and Bronon is still recovering from illness. Baurucra and Bausers have both been defeated by the British. Rakoste's performance has been greatly reduced after marriage, so he is afraid of enemies from Britain and the United States.

Women's Championship Will Fall to British Hands

Because of Mrs. Madi's absence from the women's championship, the voice of British Ms. Nat Ho is the highest. The enemies are German Ms. Olsen, American Mrs. Harper, and Spanish Ms. Taifolans, etc.

Free Talk

World Anecdotes

— Hai Ke

16,840 Types of Occupations

We Chinese commonly say there are 360 lines of business, but if you carefully count them, I'm afraid there are more than that. As for various Western countries, they are constantly innovating in everything, so there are particularly many occupations. Take England for example, it is said that there are as many as 16,840 types. Among these many occupations, there are some with strange names, such as "Powder Monkey," "Bogey Mao," and "Spout Girl." Just looking at these names, we don't know what they are. In addition, "Alley Girl" refers to women in soap factories who are responsible for reviewing soap after it has been made and stamped with a pattern. They are called Alley Girls, but it is not known where the name comes from. Another example is "Sandwich Man," which refers to people on the street who carry advertising boards. They hang two advertising boards in front of and behind their bodies, with their bodies sandwiched in between, just like a sandwich.

Insurance for Warships in Movies

A great movie company in England shot a great naval film last year. For the sake of realism, they specially borrowed ten warships from the government and asked the sailors on the ships to participate in the performance. The government approved their request, but required them to insure all the warships for 20 million gold pounds to prevent any accidents.

Strange Customs of the Taiwanese Aborigines

— Li Xu Fan

Taiwan is located in a remote corner of the sea, facing Fujian Province across the water. It is rich in products, especially sugar. Since it was ceded to Japan after the Jiawu War, it has become a strange humiliation in our country's diplomacy. Whenever our people think of this, they cannot help but feel emotional. My old friend Mr. Song is a sugar merchant who inherited his family business. He has been in Taiwan for decades. Recently, because he could not get used to the oppression of imperialism, he retired to Shanghai. When he talked about the situation there and the customs of the aborigines, he found many things laughable, and he was particularly saddened. Now, I will record what I can remember to help with conversation.

Taiwan is divided into front and back. The back is mostly inhabited by aborigines. There are distinctions between civilized and uncivilized aborigines. Those who have been civilized are called civilized aborigines, and those who have not been civilized are called uncivilized aborigines. When outsiders want to exchange goods, it is all done through the civilized aborigines. During the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty, Liu Kunyi governed Taiwan. Later, because the land in the back was vast and the resources were abundant, he planned to develop it and increase the population. Through the translation of the civilized aborigines, he sent many brave and capable men to guide cultivation. He allocated 10,000 head of cattle for plowing, along with shovels and other tools, and seeds of rice, wheat, beans, and sorghum, and earnestly advised them. Unexpectedly, the aborigines were naturally barbaric and could not be educated. As a result, they slaughtered the cattle for food and drove the officials away. After several attempts, they were still not civilized. Then, they added military force to conquer them, but the mountain roads were rugged, and these people were used to crossing the mountains and hiding in caves, so the conquest was unsuccessful. It was even more difficult to achieve results than Zhuge Liang's conquest of the Southern Barbarians. Although the uncivilized aborigines were like this, the customs of the civilized aborigines were also not easy to evolve. There was a kind of crude custom of welcoming gods and holding festivals, which was laughable to hear. Often, in the spring and summer, they gathered a group of men and women, who bared their upper bodies, had disheveled hair, and dirty feet and faces, with fierce appearances. Their lower bodies were only covered with a red and green cloth skirt, which was divided into upper and lower parts, forming a flag gate shape, just like the battle skirts of the Qing soldiers. They walked slowly on the road, exposing their buttocks. They lined up in two rows, with more than a hundred people leading the way. In the middle, they carried a bamboo sedan chair that looked like a chair, covered with red cloth like a curtain. Inside, there was a human head, dripping with fresh blood. Especially killing people from other villages was considered a good omen. Two bamboo poles were inserted on both sides of the sedan chair, and four people shared each end. When they moved, everyone shouted loudly, no different from wolves howling and apes crying. More than a hundred people followed behind the sedan chair, each holding a burning incense stick. Finally, there was a person wearing a red-topped official hat with peacock feathers and a yellow jacket, and wearing black boots. He was called the "god guard." This kind of incongruous custom only reached the realm of admiring red-topped official hats with peacock feathers. Compared to the uncivilized aborigines, it was indeed a world apart. Even if we judge the national character of the entire Taiwan, their thinking is more outdated than in other places. No wonder they have been subjected to the rule of foreign races for decades.

There is another thing that is regrettable. The opposite side of Taiwan is Nan'an in Fujian. Footprints of wooden clogs are often seen there. All the lawless Hong Kong people often use Taiwanese nationality as a protective talisman. They all paste name cards with Taiwanese nationality on the doors of their residences to secretly resist the inspection of the local authorities. My old friend Wang Yongmei once served as a police chief there, but he resigned because he was hindered in his work. Now, hearing Mr. Song's words, I am even more convinced.

A Chance Encounter Between Ma and Chen

— Wan Cheng

The famous scholars Mr. Ma Junwu and Mr. Chen Zhuzun live simple and frugal lives. Mr. Chen's eldest son is studying in the United States, and the expenses are huge. He barely manages to maintain it with the salary he receives from teaching at Jiaotong University and Great China University. Mr. Chen's life has been particularly frugal recently. One day last month, he took a third-class tram to Xujiahui to teach at Jiaotong University. It happened that Mr. Ma Junwu also boarded the third-class tram. Chen saw Ma and shouted, "You're here too." Then they talked about their feelings for a while and said that they were both in "poor" circumstances recently.

A Lesson from a Meal

— Xiao Chang

Yesterday, my friend Mr. Sun Jinfang told me about a young man's character, which is worth recording. I am now transcribing it here.

In the northern countryside of Zhuji, there is a man named Ling, who is the son of a wealthy family. When he was young, his parents loved him but did not teach him, so he did not understand the ways of the world or human feelings, and he was willful, arrogant, and impolite. His father was not ignorant of reason, but only thought that his son was used to being spoiled and could not be remedied by family education. Therefore, he planned to send his son out to study and learn business rules. Later, through a friend in Hangzhou, Mr. Lu, he was recommended to study at a certain bank in Hangzhou. On the day Ling entered the shop, he wore luxurious clothes and took a carriage from the home of the introducer, Mr. Lu, which was two li away from the bank. After arriving at the shop, he bowed to Mr. Wu Langzhai, the manager of the bank, as his teacher. Wu immediately disliked Ling when he saw him, because no apprentice who entered the shop had ever been so extravagant. After Ling entered the shop, he soon had lunch, sharing a table with his teacher. The dishes were three vegetarian and one meat. Ling was the son of a wealthy family and never ate vegetarian food for every meal. Therefore, as soon as the meal was in his mouth, he first put his chopsticks into the meat bowl. His teacher was very angry when he saw this and immediately taught him, "This is meat. Everyone at the table must put their chopsticks in the dish before you can eat it. This is the rule for apprentices when they eat." Ling was shocked by this and quickly retracted his chopsticks to pick up vegetarian dishes, and finished a bowl of rice. Then, everyone finished eating, and Ling said to his teacher, "Sir, I want to go home." Wu was surprised and said, "To study outside, you must complete three years of study before you can return home. Now you have only been here for a few hours. Why do you want to go back?" Ling said, "The reason why I came here to study is not to make a living in the future, but to learn the rules. I have just received a lesson from you at the meal, and I know that it is important to have etiquette in everything. Even small things like eating a meal require such attention. Other things go without saying. But because I received a lesson from you at the meal, I have already understood everything about how to be a person, so I don't need to stay here any longer. Although I am very grateful to you, and I am only leaving after following you for a few hours, the proverb that 'one day as a teacher, a lifetime as a student' should be forever remembered." The teacher heard this and did not know what to say. He ordered someone to call the introducer, Mr. Lu. Ling said the same thing to Lu as above. Lu repeatedly persuaded him to stay, but Ling firmly refused. Wu and Lu saw that his will was firm and his words were sincere, so they agreed. Then Ling went home.

Unexpectedly, after Ling returned home, he followed the rules and regulations and reversed his previous character. Therefore, his parents were happy, and the villagers praised him. Ling often said to people, "The reason why I was able to become like this is all thanks to my teacher, Mr. Wu Langzhai." It is said that after Ling returned home from his studies, in addition to writing letters to greet his teacher from time to time and giving him gifts, he would definitely go to Hangzhou in person every year to visit him. Ling is now forty-five years old, and his virtuous name is known throughout the village. My friend Mr. Sun is from the same village as Ling, so he knows him very well.

Interesting News from the Painting Exhibition

— Yan Zi

Mr. Sun Xueni, a famous painter in Shanghai, advocated for round fans, so he invited more than 50 painters living in Shanghai, such as Shang Shengbo, Ma Qizhou, Xie Gongzhan, He Tianjian, Xiong Songquan, Wang Shizi, and Ma Mengrong, to paint landscapes, flowers, birds, and figures, totaling more than 1,400 pieces. They held a round fan exhibition at the Ningbo Fellow Association. Those who heard the news and joined in included Ms. Li Qiujun, Lu Xiaoman, Gao Shiyun, and Yang Xuejiu, as well as the two poets Xiaodie and Jianzhi, who also displayed their most exquisite works in the exhibition. Wang Yiting, Shen Xinhai, Ye Weishen, Gao Shangzhi, and others also sent fan pieces on the second day. Old Man Zhegen was afraid that others would get there first, so he didn't sleep all night. As soon as the sky was bright, he waited at the entrance of the Fellow Association. When the door opened at seven o'clock, he went upstairs to select 24 exquisite pieces. While he was selecting, Wang Shizi and Xie Gongzhan both arrived. When they saw the fans that Zhegen had chosen, they laughed and said, "I didn't expect you to get there first." The humor was like this.

Ms. Qiujun personally sent the fans. There were dozens of people from the Ningbo Fellow Association trailing behind. They were just reviewing the paintings, and those who were deciding on the paintings were fighting with each other, and no one would give way. It was indeed a respect for her reputation. Ms. Xiaoman's paintings, as well as the fan paintings of Xiaodie and Shiyun, a total of six or seven pieces, were all snatched up by the painters. Those who arrived later all called out in regret.

For the 70th birthday celebration of Old Man Jianchao, a giant in the literary world, President Yu Youren of the National Government ordered 300 painted fans to be distributed as birthday gifts.

The painted fans of Shengbo, Qizhou, Tianjian, Gongzhan, Wuchang, Shizi, Songquan, Xueni, and Weishen were even fought over by three or four people, causing a commotion. Later, after Xueni mediated, each person decided on one fan, and the quarrel stopped. In early June, Wang Zhongshan, Zhang Yuguang, Xu Xiaocun, Gao Shangzhi, and others, a total of 13 people, initiated a fan surface exhibition. Even more people came to buy after hearing the news. There were even six or seven people who ordered the same painting on one fan. In three days, they sold more than 2,000 yuan.

Starting from the 13th, Zhao Banpo, Wu Ziding, and Ma Wanli opened a painting exhibition at the Fellow Association. I also went to visit. Banpo's paintings were priced at 15 yuan each, and they were all inscribed with poems by Pan Laolan, Zhang Lengseng, and Gao Zhenxiao, which were highly praised by the general public. I remember Pan's inscription on a peach blossom painting: "Double oars ride the tide as the sun sets, in whose alley is the small peach blossom? The roots and leaves evoke the beauty of the capital, a tree enchants, especially when it's in bloom." The style was excellent, and it could be called a perfect match with Banpo's light and elegant brushwork. The British consul Pei Jun saw it and appreciated it, and ordered four paintings. Wu's paintings were very similar to Xiao Xiaolou, and even more people ordered them. The large lotus flower painted by Wanli was purely imitated from Huishu, surpassing the master. Liang Gongyue wrote a poem: "The water of Mochou Lake is heavy with the sky, things lean on the new autumn, thoughts are lost. After the rain clears in the Zhuge Pavilion, the broken clouds and the setting sun pity each other." The three perfections of poetry, calligraphy, and painting were most admired by the visitors. More than a dozen people ordered paintings.

After Reading Mr. Cai Zhenghua's Examples of Yuan Dynasty Opera Suites

— Yun Jian Liang

Among the works in the Chinese literary world, the most exquisite, most detailed, most interesting, most moving, most widely promoted, and most valuable are opera suites. Opera suites originated from ci poetry, and ci poetry originated from the Music Bureau. However, the Music Bureau advanced to ci poetry, and ci poetry advanced to opera suites. This is the obvious and orderly formula of literary evolution. According to the Yuan Dynasty opera suites, they evolved from the great songs of the Song Dynasty and were called zaju. There were dances and songs, and the sheng, flute, and pipa were used to harmonize the music. The so-called song is the text of the zaju. There were many famous artists at that time, and Guan, Wang, Zheng, and Bai were the four great masters. Guan was like a drunken guest at a banquet, Wang was like a beauty under flowers, Zheng's voice was like jade coughing in the sky, and Bai's talent was like a Peng bird soaring in the sky. In addition, the remaining colors scattered like brocade were beautiful beyond compare. The trend of the times made it prosperous for a time. What Mr. Zhenghua described were mostly writers from the Yuan Dynasty. He had everything he should have, selecting the best and being detailed in his language, indicating the right path, so that those who study opera suites would no longer have the sigh of groping in the dark. His contribution to the opera world is not shallow. If the students who inherit his learning can trace the ci poetry from the opera suites, and study the drama from the ci poetry, chewing and discussing them, they will have high interest and deep taste, and their aesthetic understanding of writing will surely make great progress. It can be predicted that they will examine the life experiences of the writers of the time, who were subjected to the power of foreign barbarians, wrote about the suffering of the common people, and were filled with repressed and uneasy emotions in their writing, which were no different from the allegories of Ban, Ma, Sao, and Zhuang. Moreover, they were appreciated by both the refined and the vulgar, and were suitable for both ancient and modern times. How wide and deep their influence and promotion were can be compared to Gu Yong Qian Yuan Zhou. What is their structure? There are suites, and there are filler words and filler phrases. In their performances, there are distinctions between guests, dialogues, subjects, translations, beginnings, climaxes, and endings. The events are narrated in the dialogues, while the song texts are all spoken on behalf of the characters. Compared to the works of the Song and Jin Dynasties, they were indeed a step forward. The descriptions were emotional, vivid, and colorful. Their wonderful and unique points were able to make the listeners and readers lose their souls in the joys and sorrows, ups and downs of the drama, and cry or smile without being able to control themselves. Are they not extremely exquisite, detailed, difficult, and valuable? That is why I say that opera suites are the most valuable in the literary world. I was asked by Dr. Shen Siliang, the vice president of St. John's University, to review Master Zhenghua's works and planned to give him a degree. In addition to my comments, I am adding a few words to ask Mr. Wu Quan what he thinks. Written by Lu Guiliang on June 13, the 20th year of the Republic of China.

Rotary Club for Storytellers

???

— Xu Zhuo Dai

When Pan Ziliang woke up at dawn, he suddenly felt a stuffiness in his chest, as if something weighing hundreds of pounds was pressing on his body, which was very uncomfortable. He wanted to open his eyes, but the sleeping demon was still entangling him and would not let him go, so he still could not wake up. He only felt sleepy! But the weight on his chest was still pressing down. From his half-conscious state, he suddenly remembered something. He had heard a joke from a friend before: An old scholar woke up in the middle of the night and suddenly shouted for help in bed. Because he felt as if someone was tying his neck with a belt and planning to strangle him to death. Later, his wife, who shared the bed with him, woke up when she heard the noise. When she lit the lamp and took a look, it was truly a joke! It turned out that his wife's foot strap had somehow wrapped around his neck, so he was breathing rapidly and thought someone was trying to kill him, so he shouted for help. At this moment, Ziliang thought vaguely:

"My wife has natural feet and doesn't have foot straps, so of course she wouldn't make me unable to breathe. Then, what is pressing on my chest? Could it be that she is in a bad mood and put her legs on me in her sleep? That wouldn't be so heavy either..."

Just then, he suddenly felt an itch in his nose, and he was about to sneeze. This stimulation was so strong that it forcefully woke up Pan Ziliang, who was still in a deep sleep and had not yet reached his daily wake-up time.

Ziliang used all his strength to open his eyelids, which felt as if they weighed an infinite number of pounds. As soon as he opened them, but not fully, he was startled. It turned out that there was a huge face no more than three or four inches away from his eyes. This fright turned Ziliang from a semi-awake state to a fully awake state. But in the next instant, he was no longer frightened.

It turned out that this huge face was not some demon or monster, but the delicate face of his wife, Madam Yueru. He saw that her upper body was lying on his chest, no wonder it felt heavy. Her right hand was holding a hemp thread, trying to insert it into his nostril. Her face was very close, so it felt so big. As soon as she saw that Ziliang was awake, she giggled and retracted the hemp thread in her right hand.

Prices for all months fell by one tael, two mace, four fen, and seven qian. The market sentiment remained weak in the afternoon, and prices fell by another six to nine qian. The trading volume was 55,750 bales. It was found that Mei Kee sold 2,200 bales, Tong Yu 1,600 bales, Tai Chang 1,000 bales, Yi Chang 1,150 bales, Heng De 2,000 bales, Chang Feng 1,500 bales, Yi Da 1,200 bales, and Yi Yu 1,500 bales. Mei Kee bought 1,000 bales, Ji Feng 1,400 bales, Gong Tai 1,300 bales, Tian Long 900 bales, Geng Feng 2,300 bales, Yi Yu 2,350 bales, and Heng De 650 bales. The closing prices are recorded below:

Yarn Sales Are Only Average

The sales of spot yarn are relatively flat. It is found that various groups purchased a total of 1,000 bales throughout the day. Transactions among peers were 650 bales, and the market was flat. Customer groups imported 125 bales from Hankou, 200 bales from Guangdong, 250 bales from the inland, 35 bales from the northern groups, 100 bales from Shantou, 35 bales from Changsha, 70 bales from Tianjin, and 200 bales from miscellaneous groups, it is said.

Cotton Market Has Not Escaped Sluggishness

The cotton market is still sluggish, but US cotton prices are soaring. The morale in this port is not high. Because the silver market is rising, and the yarn market is not good, there is a lack of buyers, and the market disk is becoming more and more loose. However, Japanese merchants still have no intention of giving up, it is said.

Hankou Marker Down Three to Four Qian

At the opening of the Hankou Marker cotton futures market this morning, the market sentiment was very weak, and prices fell by 2.4 qian across the board. In the afternoon, the current month rose by 5 fen, while the distant months fell by another 1.5 qian. The trading volume was 81,700 dan. It was found that Shenxin sold 3,000 dan, Changfeng 4,300 dan, Shenda 2,200 dan, and Xincheng 3,800 dan. Tianlong bought 4,300 dan, Shenchang 3,400 dan, Xinheng 7,100 dan, and Xingyuan 3,100 dan. Foreign cotton yarn rises violently

US Cotton Purchasing Power Very Strong

Yesterday, US cotton soared because of mass buying, political news favorable to long positions, and strong support from Wall Street. Futures rose 67 to 71 points per pound, and spot rose 70 points per pound. British cotton futures rose 32-33 points, and spot rose 40 points. Egyptian cotton spot rose 55 points. Indian cotton was firm due to good news from Liverpool, short covering, and buying by speculators. Pingguoer and Aomula rose 6 rupees, and Bailuoxi rose 9 rupees.
